In [3]:
df['x3'] = df['x1'] ** 2
df['x4'] = df['x2'] ** 2
X = df[['x1', 'x2', 'x3', 'x4']]
y = df['class']
print(X.shape)
print(y.shape)

(12, 4)
(12,)
In [4]:
model = Sequential()
model.add(Dense(1, input_shape=(4,), activation='relu'))
In [5]:
%%time
model.compile(optimizer='adam', loss='binary_crossentropy',
              metrics=['accuracy'])
fit_log = model.fit(X, y, epochs=4000, batch_size=1)
